Source Code

This is a reconstructed version of Luminary 130, the initial AGC program released in November 1969 for the Apollo 13 LM. Three more releases followed before the flown revision was finally manufactured in February 1970.

This reconstruction was created from a previous transcription of the original listing of Luminary 131, combined with Luminary memo #129 which describes the small difference between the Luminary 130 and 131. The reconstructed source code was verified by matching memory-bank checksums to those listed for Luminary 130 in drawing 2021152G.

In this source code, program comments from the original (Luminary 131) code are prefixed with '#', while those added later by the Virtual AGC project are prefixed with '##'. 

021206,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
021207,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    P20-P25.agc
021208,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of the reconstructed source code for Luminary 130.
021209,000005:                                                                                                  ##              This was the original program released for the Apollo 13 LM,
021210,000006:                                                                                                  ##              although several more revisions would follow. It has been
021211,000007:                                                                                                  ##              reconstructed from a listing of Luminary 131, from which it
021212,000008:                                                                                                  ##              differs on only two lines in P70-P71. The difference is
021213,000009:                                                                                                  ##              described in detail in Luminary memo #129, which was used
021214,000010:                                                                                                  ##              to perform the reconstruction. This file is intended to be a
021215,000011:                                                                                                  ##              faithful reconstruction, except that the code format has been
021216,000012:                                                                                                  ##              changed to conform to the requirements of the yaYUL assembler
021217,000013:                                                                                                  ##              rather than the original YUL assembler.
021218,000014:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 496-618
021219,000015:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
021220,000016:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
021221,000017:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 05/15/03 RSB.   Began transcribing.
021222,000018:                                                                                                  ##              12/01/03 RSB.   Entered/corrected the previously-missing code from
021223,000019:                                                                                                  ##                              the bottom of p. 595 using a replacement scan
021224,000020:                                                                                                  ##                              provided by Gary Neff.
021225,000021:                                                                                                  ##              05/14/05 RSB    Corrected website reference above.
021226,000022:                                                                                                  ##              2010-10-25 JL   Fixed p583 page number.
021227,000023:                                                                                                  ##              2011-05-07 JL   Removed workarounds.
021228,000024:                                                                                                  ##              2017-01-06 RSB  Page numbers now agree with those on the
021229,000025:                                                                                                  ##                              original harcopy, as opposed to the PDF page
021230,000026:                                                                                                  ##                              numbers in 1701.pdf.
021231,000027:                                                                                                  ##              2017-01-28 RSB  WTIH -> WITH.
021232,000028:                                                                                                  ##              2017-02-24 RSB  Proofed comment text using octopus/ProoferComments.
021233,000029:                                                                                                  ##              2017-02-28 RSB  Fixed lingering typos.

021243,000039:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
021244,000040: 
021245,000041:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021246,000042: 
021247,000043:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021248,000044:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021249,000045: 
021250,000046:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021251,000047: 
021252,000048:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO CONTROL THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR FROM
021253,000049:                                                                                                  #        STARTUP THROUGH ACQUISITION AND LOCKON TO THE CSM AND TO UPDATE EITHER 
021254,000050:                                                                                                  #        THE LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (AS SPECIFIED BY THE ASTRONAUT BY DSKY ENTRY)
021255,000051:                                                                                                  #        ON THE BASIS OF THE RR TRACKING DATA.
021256,000052: 
021257,000053:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021258,000054: 
021259,000055:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E20E
021260,000056: 
021261,000057:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
021262,000058: 
021263,000059:                                                                                                  #        R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)                      FLAGUP
021264,000060:                                                                                                  #        GOFLASH (PINBALL-DISPLAY)                       FLAGDOWN
021265,000061:                                                                                                  #        R23LEM  (MANUAL ACQUISITION)                    BANKCALL
021266,000062:                                                                                                  #        LS201   (LOS DETERMINATION)                     TASKOVER
021267,000063:                                                                                                  #        LS202   (RANGE LIMIT TEST)
021268,000064:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM  (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
021269,000065:                                                                                                  #        R21LEM  (RR DESIGNATE)                          ENDOFJOB
021270,000066:                                                                                                  #        R22LEM  (DATA READ)                             GOPERF1
021271,000067:                                                                                                  #        R31LEM  (RENDEZVOUS PARAMETER DISPLAY)  
021272,000068:                                                                                                  #        PRIOLARM (PRIORITY DISPLAY)
021273,000069: 
021274,000070:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
021275,000071: 
021276,000072:                                                                                                  #        P20 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS - ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
021277,000073:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
021278,000074: 
021279,000075:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
021280,000076: 
021281,000077:                                                                                                  #        RANGE GREATER THAN 400 NM DISPLAY
021282,000078: 
021283,000079:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021284,000080: 
021285,000081:                                                                                                  #        TRKMKCNT = NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS TAKEN (COUNTER)
021286,000082: 
021287,000083:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021288,000084: 
021289,000085:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021290,000086: 
021291,000087:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, RNDVZFLG, ACMODFLG, VEHUPFLG, UPDATFLG, TRACKFLG,
021292,000088: 
021293,000089:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021294,000090: 
021295,000091:                                                                                                  #        CENTRALS - A,Q,L
021296,000092: 
021297,000093: 25,2073  30,2000                                  SBANK=   LOWSUPER                              #  FOR LOW 2CADR'S.
021298,000094: 
021299,000095: 33,2045                                           BANK     33

021301,000097: 24,2000                                           BANK

021711,000507:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021712,000508: 
021713,000509:                                                                                                  #        PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE PROGRAM P25
021714,000510:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 3

021716,000512: 
021717,000513:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021718,000514: 
021719,000515:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING
021720,000516:                                                                                                  #        ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO CONTINUOUSLY POINT THE LM TRACKING BEACON AT THE
021721,000517:                                                                                                  #        CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE AND

022020,000816:                                                                                                  #  RR DESIGNATE ROUTINE (R21LEM)
022021,000817:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022022,000818: 
022023,000819:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
022024,000820:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
022025,000821: 
022026,000822:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022027,000823: 
022028,000824:                                                                                                  #        TO POINT THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR AT THE CSM UNTIL AUTOMATIC ACQUISITION
022029,000825:                                                                                                  #        OF THE CSM IS ACCOMPLISHED BY THE RADAR.  ROUTINE IS CALLED BY P20.
022030,000826: 
022031,000827:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022032,000828: 
022033,000829:                                                                                                  #        TC      BANKCALL
022034,000830:                                                                                                  #        CADR    R21LEM
022035,000831: 
022036,000832:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
022037,000833: 
022038,000834:                                                                                                  #        FINDVAC         FLAGUP          ENDOFJOB        PRIOLARM
022039,000835:                                                                                                  #        NOVAC           INTPRET         LPS20.1         PHASCHNG
022040,000836:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST        JOBSLEEP        JOBWAKE         FLAGDOWN
022041,000837:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER        BANKCALL        RADSTALL        RRDESSM
022042,000838: 
022043,000839:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
022044,000840:                                                                                                  #        
022045,000841:                                                                                                  #        WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED, BRANCH WILL BE TO P20 WHERE R22 (DATA READ
022046,000842:                                                                                                  #        WILL BE SELECTED OR A NEED FOR A MANEUVER (BRANCH TO P20LEMA)
022047,000843: 
022048,000844:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022049,000845: 
022050,000846:                                                                                                  #        PRIORITY ALARM 503 WHEN LOCK-ON HASN:T BEEN ACHIEVED AFTER 30SECS -
022051,000847:                                                                                                  #        THIS REQUIRES ASTRONAUT INTERFACE- SELECTION OF SEARCH OPTION OF
022052,000848:                                                                                                  #        ACQUISITION
022053,000849: 
022054,000850:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022055,000851: 
022056,000852:                                                                                                  #        SEE LPS20.1, RRDESSM
022057,000853: 
022058,000854:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022059,000855: 
022060,000856:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES ARE USED BY LPS20.1 AND RRDESSM
022061,000857: 
022062,000858:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET

022065,000861:

022247,001043:                                                                                                  #  MANUAL ACQUISITION ROUTINE R23LEM
022248,001044:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022249,001045: 
022250,001046:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
022251,001047:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
022252,001048: 
022253,001049:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022254,001050: 
022255,001051:                                                                                                  #        TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY MANUAL OPERATION OF THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022256,001052: 
022257,001053:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022258,001054: 
022259,001055:                                                                                                  #        TC      R23LEM
022260,001056: 
022261,001057:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022262,001058: 
022263,001059:                                                                                                  #        BANKCALL        R61LEM
022264,001060:                                                                                                  #        SETMINDB        GOPERF1
022265,001061: 
022266,001062:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
022267,001063: 
022268,001064:                                                                                                  #        IN RESPONSE TO THE GOPERF1      ,SELECTION OF ENTER WILL RECYCLE R23
022269,001065:                                                                                                  #                                        ,SELECTION OF PROC WILL CONTINUE R23
022270,001066:                                                                                                  #                                        ,SELECTION OF TERM WILL TERMINATE R23 + P20
022271,001067: 
022272,001068:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022273,001069: 
022274,001070:                                                                                                  #        SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
022275,001071: 
022276,001072:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022277,001073: 
022278,001074:                                                                                                  #        N.A.
022279,001075: 
022280,001076:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED -
022281,001077: 
022282,001078:                                                                                                  #        ACMODFLG MUST BE SET TO 1 (MANUAL MODE)
022283,001079: 
022284,001080: 24,3137     1142                                  EBANK=   GENRET                                
022285,001081: 24,3137                                           COUNT*   $$/R23                                
022286,001082: 24,3137           05504        R23LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                #  SET NO ANGLE MONITOR FLAG
022287,001083: 24,3140           00126                           ADRES    NORRMON                               
022288,001084: 24,3141           00004                           INHINT                                         
022289,001085: 24,3142           04674                           TC       IBNKCALL                              #  SELECT MINIMUM DEADBAND
022290,001086: 24,3143           40141                           CADR     SETMINDB                              
022291,001087: 24,3144           00003                           RELINT                                         
022292,001088: 24,3145           34736        R23LEM1            CAF      BIT14                                 #  ENABLE TRACKER
022293,001089: 24,3146           00006                           EXTEND                                         
022294,001090: 24,3147           05012                           WOR      CHAN12                                
022295,001091: 24,3150           33207                           CAF      OCT205                                
022296,001092: 24,3151           04616                           TC       BANKCALL                              
022297,001093: 24,3152           20624                           CADR     GOPERF1

022331,001127:                                                                                                  #  SEARCH ROUTINE R24LEM
022332,001128:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022333,001129: 
022334,001130:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
022335,001131:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
022336,001132: 
022337,001133:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022338,001134: 
022339,001135:                                                                                                  #        TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY A SEARCH PATTERN WHEN THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR HAS
022340,001136:                                                                                                  #        FAILED TO ACQUIRE THE CSM IN THE AUTOMATIC TRACKING MODE AND TO ALLOW
022341,001137:                                                                                                  #        THE ASTRONAUT TO CONFIRM THAT REACQUISITION HAS NOT BEEN BY SIDELOBE.
022342,001138: 
022343,001139:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
022344,001140: 
022345,001141:                                                                                                  #        CAF     PRIONN
022346,001142:                                                                                                  #        TC      FINDVAC
022347,001143:                                                                                                  #        EBANK=  DATAGOOD
022348,001144:                                                                                                  #        2CADR   R24LEM
022349,001145: 
022350,001146:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022351,001147: 
022352,001148:                                                                                                  #        FLAGUP          FLAGDOWN        BANKCALL
022353,001149:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM          GOFLASHR        FINDVAC
022354,001150:                                                                                                  #        ENDOFJOB        NOVAC           LSR24.1
022355,001151: 
022356,001152:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
022357,001153: 
022358,001154:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT RESPONSE TO DISPLAY OF OMEGA AND DATAGOOD.  HE CAN EITHER
022359,001155:                                                                                                  #        REJECT BY TERMINATING (SEARCH OPTION AND RESELECTING P20) OR ACCEPT BY
022360,001156:                                                                                                  #        PROCEEDING (EXIT ROUTINE AND RETURN TO AUTO MODE IN P20)
022361,001157: 
022362,001158:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022363,001159: 
022364,001160:                                                                                                  #        SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
022365,001161: 
022366,001162:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
022367,001163: 
022368,001164:                                                                                                  #        SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR24.1 + R61LEM
022369,001165: 
022370,001166:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022371,001167: 
022372,001168:                                                                                                  #        SEE INPUT FOR LSR24.1
022373,001169: 
022374,001170:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022375,001171: 
022376,001172:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, ACMODFLG
022377,001173: 
022378,001174: 24,3210  E7,1733                                  EBANK=   DATAGOOD                              
022379,001175: 24,3210                                           COUNT*   $$/R24                                
022380,001176: 24,3210           05504        R24LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                
022381,001177: 24,3211           00037                           ADRES    SRCHOPTN                              #  SET SRCHOPT FLAG
022382,001178: 24,3212           05516                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              #  RESET LOS BEING COMPUTED FLAG TO MAKE
022383,001179: 24,3213           00041                           ADRES    LOSCMFLG                              #  SURE DODES DOESN'T GO TO R21
022384,001180: 24,3214           34755        R24LEM1            CAF      ZERO                                  
022385,001181: 24,3215           55733                           TS       DATAGOOD                              #  ZERO OUT DATA INDICATOR
022386,001182: 24,3216           55734                           TS       OMEGAD                                #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS
022387,001183: 24,3217           55735                           TS       OMEGAD     +1                         #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS
022388,001184: 24,3220           05353        R24LEM2            TC       PHASCHNG                              
022389,001185: 24,3221           04022                           OCT      04022                                 
022390,001186: 24,3222           33255                           CAF      V16N80

022676,001472:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_ RRLIMCHK                        ARE IN THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.
022677,001473: 
022678,001474:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022679,001475: 
022680,001476:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK CHECKS RR DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN
022681,001477:                                                                                                  #        THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.  INITIALLY THE DESIRED TRUNNION AND
022682,001478:                                                                                                  #        SHAFT ANGLES ARE STORED IN ITEMP1 AND ITEMP2.  THE CURRENT RR
022683,001479:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNAE MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED WHICH IS = 0 FOR
022684,001480:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 AND =1 FOR MODE 2.
022685,001481: 
022686,001482:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 - THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022687,001483:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -55 AND +55 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN LIMITS,
022688,001484:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN -70 AND +59 DEGREES.
022689,001485:                                                                                                  #        IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN TO L +3.
022690,001486: 
022691,001487:                                                                                                  #        MODE 2 - THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022692,001488:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -139 AND -25 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN
022693,001489:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS, THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN +125
022694,001490:                                                                                                  #        AND -125 (+235) DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN
022695,001491:                                                                                                  #        TO L +3.
022696,001492: 
022697,001493:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022698,001494: 
022699,001495:                                                                                                  #        L  TC  RRLIMCHK (WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED)
022700,001496:                                                                                                  #        L  +1  ADRES  T,S  (DESIRED TRUNNION ANGLE ADDRESS)
022701,001497: 
022702,001498:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022703,001499: 
022704,001500:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, MODEA, MODEB (OR DESIRED TRUNNION AND SHAFT
022705,001501:                                                                                                  #        ANGLES ELSEWHERE IN CONSECUTIVE LOCATIONS - UNSWITCHED ERASABLE OR
022706,001502:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT EBANK).
022707,001503: 
022708,001504:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_   MAGSUB
022709,001505: 
022710,001506:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
022711,001507: 
022712,001508:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
022713,001509: 
022714,001510:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_         L + 2   (EITHER OR BOTH ANGLES NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
022715,001511:                                                                                                  #                L + 3   (BOTH ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
022716,001512: 
022717,001513:    4523           00006        RRLIMCHK           EXTEND

022760,001556:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_ SETTRKF                                                 . IF EITHER:
022761,001557: 
022762,001558:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022763,001559:                                                                                                  #        SETTRKF UPDATES THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP ON THE DSKY.              HER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION.
022764,001560:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY THE LAMP TEST FLAG (IMODES33 BIT 1) IS CHECKED.
022765,001561:                                                                                                  #        IF A LAMP TEST IS IN PROGRESS, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L +1.
022766,001562:                                                                                                  #        IF NO LAMP TEST THE FOLLOWING IS CHECKED SEQUENTIALLY_
022767,001563:                                                                                                  #                1) RR CDU:S BEING ZEROED, RR CDU OK, AND RR NOT IN
022768,001564:                                                                                                  #                   AUTO MODE (RADMODES BITS 13, 7, 2).
022769,001565:                                                                                                  #                2) LR VEL DATA FAIL AND NO LR POS DATA (RADMODES BITS
022770,001566:                                                                                                  #                   8,5)
022771,001567:                                                                                                  #                3) NO RR DATA (RADMODES BIT 4)
022772,001568:                                                                                                  #        THE ABSENCE OF ALL THREE SIMULTANEOUSLY IN (1), THE PRESENCE OF BOTH
022773,001569:                                                                                                  #        IN (2), AND THE PRESENCE OF (3) RESULTS IN EITHER THE TRACKER FAIL
022774,001570:                                                                                                  #        LAMP (DSPTAB +11D BIT 8) BEING TURNED ON OR LEFT ON. OTHERWISE,
022775,001571:                                                                                                  #        THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED OFF OR IS LEFT OFF. THEREFORE, THE
022776,001572:                                                                                                  #        TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED ON IF_
022777,001573:                                                                                                  #                A) RR CDU FAILED WITH RR IN AUTO MODE AND RR CDU:S NOT BEING ZEROED.
022778,001574:                                                                                                  #                B) N SAMPLES OF LR DATA COULD NOT BE TAKEN IN 2N TRIES WITH
022779,001575:                                                                                                  #                   EITHER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION
022780,001576:                                                                                                  #                C) N SAMPLES OF RR DATA COULD NOT BE OBTAINED FROM 2N TRIES
022781,001577:                                                                                                  #                   WITH EITHER THE AL

022832,001628:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRTURNON
022833,001629: 
022834,001630:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022835,001631: 
022836,001632:                                                                                                  #        RRTURNON IS THE TURN-ON SEQUENCE WHICH, ALONG WITH
022837,001633:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB, ZEROS THE CDU:S AND DETERMINES THE RR MODE.
022838,001634:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RRZEROSB FOR THE
022839,001635:                                                                                                  #        ACTUAL TURN-ON SEQUENCE.  UPON RETURN THE PROGRAM
022840,001636:                                                                                                  #        WAITS 1 SECOND BEFORE REMOVING THE TURN-ON FLAG
022841,001637:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT1) SO THE REPOSITION ROUTINE WON:T
022842,001638:                                                                                                  #        INITIATE PROGRAM ALARM 00501.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE
022843,001639:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF A PROGRAM IS USING THE RR (STATE BIT 7).  IF
022844,001640:                                                                                                  #        SO, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR SO THAT THE RR CDU
022845,001641:                                                                                                  #        FAIL FLAG (RADMODES BIT 7) CAN BE CHECKED BEFORE
022846,001642:                                                                                                  #        RETURNING TO THE WAITING PROGRAM.  IF NOT, THE PROGRAM EXITS
022847,001643:                                                                                                  #        TO TASKOVER.
022848,001644: 
022849,001645:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  WAITLIST TASK FROM RRAUTCHK IF THE RR POWER ON AUTO
022850,001646:                                                                                                  #  BIT (CHAN 33 BIT 2) CHANGES TO 0 AND NO PROGRAM WAS USING 
022851,001647:                                                                                                  #  THE RR (STATE BIT 7).
022852,001648: 
022853,001649:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022854,001650: 
022855,001651:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, STATE
022856,001652: 
022857,001653:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  RRZEROSB, FIXDELAY, TASKOVER, ENDRADAR
022858,001654: 
022859,001655:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022860,001656:                                                                                                  #        
022861,001657:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022862,001658: 
022863,001659:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE (SEE RRZEROSB)
022864,001660: 
022865,001661:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, ENDRADAR (WAITING PROGRAM)
022866,001662: 
022867,001663: 24,3256                                           BANK     24                                    
022868,001664: 25,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S1                                 
022869,001665: 25,2000                                           BANK

022881,001677:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRZEROSB
022882,001678: 
022883,001679:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022884,001680: 
022885,001681:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB IS A CLOSED SUBROUTINE TO ZERO THE RR CDU:S,
022886,001682:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINE THE RR MODE, AND TURNS ON THE TRACKER FAIL
022887,001683:                                                                                                  #        LAMP IF REQUIRED.  INITIALLY THE RR CDU ZERO BIT (CHAN 12
022888,001684:                                                                                                  #        BIT 1) IS SET.  FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT, THE LGC
022889,001685:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU COUNTERS (OPTY, OPTX) ARE SET = 0 AFTER 
022890,001686:                                                                                                  #        WHICH THE RR CDU ZERO DISCRETE (CHAN 12 BIT 1) IS
022891,001687:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A 4 SECOND WAIT IS SET TO ALL THE RR CDU:S
022892,001688:                                                                                                  #        TO REPEAT THE ACTUAL TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES.  THE
022893,001689:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU ZERO FLAG (RADMODES BIT 13) IS REMOVED.  THE
022894,001690:                                                                                                  #        CONTENTS OF OPTY IS THEN CHECKED TO SEE IF THE TRUNNION
022895,001691:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE IS LESS THAN 90 DEGREES.  IF NOT, BIT 12 OF
022896,001692:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES IS SET = 1 TO INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 2.
022897,001693:                                                                                                  #        IF LESS THAN 90 DEGREES, BIT 12 OF RADMODES IS SET = 0 TO
022898,001694:                                                                                                  #        INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 1.  SETTRKF IS THEN CALLED TO
022899,001695:                                                                                                  #        SEE IF THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP SHOULD BE TURNED ON.
022900,001696: 
022901,001697:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  L  TC  RRZEROSB  (FROM RRTURNON AND RRZERO)
022902,001698: 
022903,001699:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022904,001700: 
022905,001701:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES (BIT 13 SET), DSPTAB +11D
022906,001702: 
022907,001703:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  FIXDELAY, MAGSUB, SETTRKF
022908,001704: 
022909,001705:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_

022911,001707:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022912,001708: 
022913,001709:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL
022914,001710: 
022915,001711:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L +1 (ALWAYS)
022916,001712:

022920,001716: 25,2105           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  COMING HERE.

022958,001754:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DORREPOS
022959,001755: 
022960,001756:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022961,001757: 
022962,001758:                                                                                                  #        DORREPOS IS A SEQUENCE OF TASKS TO DRIVE THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022963,001759:                                                                                                  #        TO A SAFE POSITION.  INITIALLY SETRRECR IS CALLED WHERE THE RR
022964,001760:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTERS (CHAN 12 BIT 2) ARE ENABLED AND LASTYCMD
022965,001761:                                                                                                  #        AND LASTXCMD SET = 0 TO INDICATE THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE
022966,001762:                                                                                                  #        DESIRED STATE AND PRESENT STATE OF THE COMMANDS.  THE RR
022967,001763:                                                                                                  #        TURN-ON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 1) IS CHECKED AND IF NOT PRESENT,
022968,001764:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM ALARM 00501 IS REQUESTED BEFORE CONTINUING.  IN EITHER
022969,001765:                                                                                                  #        CASE, FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT THE PROGRAM CHECKS THE CURRENT
022970,001766:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE (RADMODES BIT 12).  RRTONLY IS THEN CALLED
022971,001767:                                                                                                  #        TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO 180
022972,001768:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  UPON RETURN, THE CURRENT RR ANTENNA
022973,001769:                                                                                                  #        MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS AGAIN CHECKED.  RRSONLY IS THEN
022974,001770:                                                                                                  #        CALLED TO DRIVE THE SHAFT ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO
022975,001771:                                                                                                  #        -90 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  IF DURING RRTONLY OR RRSONLY A
022976,001772:                                                                                                  #        REMODE HAS BEEN REQUESTED (RADMODES BIT 14), AND ALWAYS
022977,001773:                                                                                                  #        FOLLOWING COMPLETION OF RRSONLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO
022978,001774:                                                                                                  #        REPOSRPT.  HERE THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS 
022979,001775:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE ON THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
022980,001776:                                                                                                  #        BIT 10).  IF PRESENT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO BEGDES.  IF NOT PRESENT
022981,001777:                                                                                                  #        INDICATING NO FURTHER ANTENNA CONTROL REQUIRED, THE RR ERROR
022982,001778:                                                                                                  #        COUNTER BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS REMOVED AND THE ROUTINE EXITS TO
022983,001779:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER.
022984,001780: 
022985,001781:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022986,001782: 
022987,001783:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST CALL FROM RRGIMON IF TRUNNION AND SHAFT CDU ANGLES
022988,001784:                                                                                                  #        NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE.
022989,001785: 
022990,001786:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022991,001787: 
022992,001788:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES
022993,001789: 
022994,001790:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
022995,001791: 
022996,001792:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, BEGDES (EXIT)
022997,001793: 
022998,001794:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022999,001795: 
023000,001796:                                                                                                  #        NONE
023001,001797:

023003,001799:

023051,001847:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  REMODE                                                 IVES SHAFT TO -45, AND FINALLY DRIVES
023052,001848: 
023053,001849:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                               S DONE WITH SINGLE AXIS ROTATIONS (SEE
023054,001850:                                                                                                  #        REMODE IS THE GENERAL REMODING SUBROUTINE.  IT DRIVES THE
023055,001851:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF THE CURRENT MODE IS MODE 1,
023056,001852:                                                                                                  #        180 DEGREES FOR MODE 2, THEN DRIVES THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45
023057,001853:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES, AND FINALLY DRIVES THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130 DEGREES,
023058,001854:                                                                                                  #        TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2, -50 DEGREES FOR MODE 1, BEFORE
023059,001855:                                                                                                  #        INITIATING 2-AXIS CONTROL.  ALL REMODING IS DONE WITH SINGLE
023060,001856:                                                                                                  #        AXIS ROTATIONS (RR1AXIS).  INITIALLY THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
023061,001857:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED.  CONTROL IS THEN TRANSFERRED TO
023062,001858:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY TO DRIVE THR TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1
023063,001859:                                                                                                  #        OR 180 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  RRSONLY IS THEN CALLED TO DRIVE
023064,001860:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45 DEGREES. THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
023065,001861:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED AGAIN.  CONTROL IS AGAIN
023066,001862:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO RRTONLY TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130
023067,001863:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2 IF CURRENTLY IN MODE 1 OR TO
023068,001864:                                                                                                  #        -50 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2 TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 1.  RMODINV
023069,001865:                                                                                                  #        IS THEN CALLED TO SET RADMODES BIT 12 TO INDICATE THE NEW
023070,001866:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE.  THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14)
023071,001867:                                                                                                  #        IS REMOVED TO INDICATE THAT REMODING IS COMPLETE.  THE PROGRAM
023072,001868:                                                                                                  #        THEN EXITS TO STDESIG TO BEGIN 2-AXIS CONTROL.
023073,001869: 
023074,001870:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023075,001871: 
023076,001872:                                                                                                  #        FROM BEGDES WHEN REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) IS SET.
023077,001873:                                                                                                  #        THIS FLAG MAY BE SET IN RRDESSM AND RRDESNB IF RRLIMCHK
023078,001874:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINES THAT THE DESIRED ANGLES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
023079,001875:                                                                                                  #        OTHER MODE.
023080,001876: 
023081,001877:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023082,001878: 
023083,001879:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES
023084,001880: 
023085,001881:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023086,001882: 
023087,001883:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, RMODINV (ACTUALLY PART OF)
023088,001884: 
023089,001885:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023090,001886: 
023091,001887:                                                                                                  #        NONE
023092,001888: 
023093,001889:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE

023147,001943:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAMES_        RRTONLY, RRSONLY
023148,001944: 
023149,001945:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023150,001946: 
023151,001947:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE SUBROUTINES FOR DOING SINGLE AXIS
023152,001948:                                                                                                  #        RRMANEUVERS FOR REMODE AND REPOSITION.  IT DRIVES TO
023153,001949:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  INITIALLY, AT RR1AX2, THE REMODE AND REPOSITION
023154,001950:                                                                                                  #        FLAGS (RADMODES BITS 14, 11) ARE CHECKED.  IF BOTH EXIST,
023155,001951:                                                                                                  #        THE PROGRAM EXITS TO REPOSRPT (SEE DORREPOS).  THIS INDICATES
023156,001952:                                                                                                  #        THAT SOMEONE POSSIBLY REQUESTED A DESIGNATE (RADMODES BIT 10)
023157,001953:                                                                                                  #        WHICH REQUIRES A REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) AND THAT A
023158,001954:                                                                                                  #        REPOSITION IS IN PROGRESS (RADMODES BIT 11).  IF NONE
023159,001955:                                                                                                  #        OR ONLY ONE OF THE FLAGS EXIST, REMODE OR REPOSITION, MAGSUB
023160,001956:                                                                                                  #        IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE APPROPRIATE ANGLE IS WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  IF YES,
023161,001957:                                                                                                  #        CONTROL RETURNS TO THE CALLING ROUTINE.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS
023162,001958:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO RROUT FOR SINGLE AXIS MANEUVERS WITH THE OTHER
023163,001959:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE SET = 0.  FOLLOWING A .5 SECOND WAIT, THE ABOVE PROCEDURE IS
023164,001960:                                                                                                  #        REPEATED.
023165,001961: 
023166,001962:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:     L-1     CAF     *ANGLE*         (DESIRED ANGLE SCALED PI)
023167,001963:                                                                                                  #                        L       TC      RRTONLY         (TRUNNION ONLY)
023168,001964:                                                                                                  #                        RRSONLY                         (SHAFT ONLY)
023169,001965:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY IS CALLED BY PREPOS29;
023170,001966:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE CALLED BY DORREPOS AND REMODE
023171,001967: 
023172,001968:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023173,001969: 
023174,001970:                                                                                                  #        C(A) = DESIRED ANGLE, RADMODES
023175,001971: 
023176,001972:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023177,001973: 
023178,001974:                                                                                                  #        FIXDELAY, REPOSRPT, MAGSUB, RROUT
023179,001975: 
023180,001976:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023181,001977: 
023182,001978:                                                                                                  #        NONE
023183,001979: 
023184,001980:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023185,001981: 
023186,001982:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_ REPOSRPT (REMODE AND REPOSITION FLAGS PRESENT - RADMODES
023187,001983:                                                                                                  #        BITS 14, 11)
023188,001984:                                                                                                  #        L+1 (ANGLE WITHIN ONE DEGREE OR RR OUT OF AUTO MODE)
023189,001985: 
023190,001986: 25,2252           55313        RRTONLY            TS       RDES                                  #  DESIRED TRUNION ANGLE.

023239,002035:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RROUT                                          RROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT LIMITS THEM
023240,002036: 
023241,002037:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023242,002038: 
023243,002039:                                                                                                  #        RROUT RECEIVES RR GYRO COMMANDS IN TANG, TANG +1 IN RR
023244,002040:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTER SCALING.  RROUT THEN LIMITS THEM AND
023245,002041:                                                                                                  #        GENERATES COMMANDS TO THE CDU TO ADJUST THE ERROR COUNTERS
023246,002042:                                                                                                  #        TO THE DESIRED VALUES.  INITIALLY MAGSUB CHECKS THE MAGNITUDE OF
023247,002043:                                                                                                  #        THE COMMAND (SHAFT ON 1ST PASS) TO SEE IF IT IS GREATER THAN
023248,002044:                                                                                                  #        384 PULSES.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RROUTLIM TO
023249,002045:                                                                                                  #        LIMIT THE COMMAND TO +384 OR -384 PULSES.  THE DIFFERENCE IS
023250,002046:                                                                                                  #        THEN CALCULATED BETWEEN THE DESIRED STATE AND THE PRESENT STATE OF
023251,002047:                                                                                                  #        THE ERROR COUNTER AS RECORDED IN LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD.
023252,002048:                                                                                                  #        THE RESULT IS STORED IN OPTXCMD (1ST PASS) AND OPTYCMD (2ND
023253,002049:                                                                                                  #        PASS).  FOLLOWING THE SECOND PASS, FOR THE TRUNNION COMMAND, THE
023254,002050:                                                                                                  #        OCDUT AND OCDUS ERROR COUNTER DRIVE BITS (CHAN 14 BITS 12, 11)
023255,002051:                                                                                                  #        ARE SET.  THIS PROGRAM THEN EXITS TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.
023256,002052: 
023257,002053:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023258,002054:                                                                                                  #        
023259,002055:                                                                                                  #        L TC RROUT (WITH RUPT INHIBITED) RROUT IS CALLED BY
023260,002056:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, AND DODES
023261,002057: 
023262,002058:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023263,002059: 
023264,002060:                                                                                                  #        TANG, TANG +1 (DESIRED COMMANDS), LASTYCMD, LASTXCMD
023265,002061:                                                                                                  #        (1ST PASS = 0), RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE SET (CHAN 12 BIT 2).
023266,002062:

023349,002145:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRDESSM                                                R (HALF-UNIT) IN RRTARGET. REMODES IF
023350,002146: 
023351,002147:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023352,002148: 
023353,002149:                                                                                                  #        THIS INTERPRETIVE ROUTINE WILL DESIGNATE, IF DESIRED ANGLES ARE
023354,002150:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN THE LIMITS OF EITHER MODE, TO A LINE-OF SIGHT (LOS) VECTOR
023355,002151:                                                                                                  #        (HALF-UNIT) KNOWN WITH RESPECT TO THE STABLE MEMBER PRESENT
023356,002152:                                                                                                  #        ORIENTATION.  INITIALLY THE IMU CDU:S ARE READ AND CONTROL
023357,002153:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO SMNB TO TRANSFORM THE LOS VECTOR FROM STABLE
023358,002154:                                                                                                  #        MEMBER TO NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES (SEE STG MEMO -699)
023359,002155:                                                                                                  #        RRANGLES IS THEN CALLED TO CALCULATE THE RR GIMBAL ANGLES,
023360,002156:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION AND SHAFT, FOR BOTH THE PRESENT AND ALTERNATE MODE.
023361,002157:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE
023362,002158:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT MODE ARE WITHIN LIMITS.  IF WITHIN LIMITS, THE RETURN
023363,002159:                                                                                                  #        LOCATION IS INCREMENTED, INASMUCH AS NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS
023364,002160:                                                                                                  #        REQUIRED, BEFORE EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF THE
023365,002161:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT MODE, TRYSWS IS CALLED.  FOLLOWING INVERTING OF THE RR
023366,002162:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 12), RRLIMCHK IS CALLED
023367,002163:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE ALTERNATE MODE ARE WITHIN
023368,002164:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS.  IF YES, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG IS AGAIN INVERTED,
023369,002165:                                                                                                  #        THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) SET, AND THE RETURN LOCATION
023370,002166:                                                                                                  #        INCREMENTED, TO INDICATE NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED, BEFORE
023371,002167:                                                                                                  #        EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF THESE ANGLES ARE NOT WITHIN LIMITS
023372,002168:                                                                                                  #        OF THE ALTERNATE MODE, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES
023373,002169:                                                                                                  #        BIT 12) IS INVERTED BEFORE RETURNING DIRECTLY TO THE CALLING PROGRAM
023374,002170:                                                                                                  #        TO INDICATE THAT A VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED.
023375,002171: 
023376,002172:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023377,002173: 
023378,002174:                                                                                                  #        L       STCALL  RRTARGET        (LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN SM COORDINATES)
023379,002175:                                                                                                  #        L+1     RRDESSM
023380,002176:                                                                                                  #        L+2     BASIC                   (VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023381,002177:                                                                                                  #        L+3     BASIC                   (NO VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023382,002178: 
023383,002179:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023384,002180: 
023385,002181:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES
023386,002182: 
023387,002183:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023388,002184: 
023389,002185:                                                                                                  #        READCDUS, SMNB, RRANGLES, RRLIMCHK, TRYSWS (ACTUALLY
023390,002186:                                                                                                  #        PART OF), RMODINV
023391,002187: 
023392,002188:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023393,002189: 
023394,002190:                                                                                                  #        NONE
023395,002191: 
023396,002192:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023397,002193: 
023398,002194:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L+2 (NEITHER SET OF ANGLES ARE WITHIN LIMITS OF RELATED MODE)
023399,002195:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES (DESIGNATE POSSIBLE AT PRESENT VEHICLE ATTITUDE-RETURNS
023400,002196:                                                                                                  #  TO L+3 FROM STARTDES)                                                 CAN BE DONE IN PRESENT VEH ATTITUDE.
023401,002197: 
023402,002198: 25,2404           43020        RRDESSM            STQ      CLEAR                                 
023403,002199: 25,2405           01112                                    DESRET

023439,002235:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  STARTDES                                                       STORED AS A HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN RRTARGET
023440,002236: 
023441,002237:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                       CKON IS DESIRED. BIT14 OF RADMODES IS
023442,002238:                                                                                                  #        STARTDES IS ENTERED WHEN WE ARE READY TO BEGIN DESIGNATION.             OR REPOSITION OPERATION. IN THIS
023443,002239:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14 OF RADMODES IS ALREADY SET IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED.              THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
023444,002240:                                                                                                  #        AT THIS TIME, THE RR ANTENNA MAY BE IN A REPOSITION                     GINS.
023445,002241:                                                                                                  #        OPERATION.  IN THIS CASE, IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED IT MAY HAVE
023446,002242:                                                                                                  #        ALREADY BEGUN BUT IN ANY CASE THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
023447,002243:                                                                                                  #        OTHERWISE, THE REPOSITION WILL BE COMPLETED BEFORE 2-AXIS
023448,002244:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATION BEGINS.  INITIALLY DESCOUNT IS SET = 60 TO INDICATE
023449,002245:                                                                                                  #        THAT 30 SECONDS WILL BE ALLOWED FOR THE RR DATA GOOD INBIT
023450,002246:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 33 BIT 4) IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED (STATE BIT 5).  BIT 10
023451,002247:                                                                                                  #        OF RADMODES IS SET TO SHOW THAT A DESIGNATE IS REQUIRED.
023452,002248:                                                                                                  #        THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED.  IF SET,
023453,002249:                                                                                                  #        THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESSM
023454,002250:                                                                                                  #        AND RRDESNB).  THE PROGRAM WILL BEGIN DESIGNATING TO THE DESIRED
023455,002251:                                                                                                  #        ANGLES FOLLOWING THE REPOSITION OR REMODE IF ONE WAS
023456,002252:                                                                                                  #        REQUESTED.  IF THE REPOSITION FLAG IS NOT SET, SETRRECR IS CALLED
023457,002253:                                                                                                  #        WHICH SETS THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2)
023458,002254:                                                                                                  #        AND SETS LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD = 0 TO INDICATE THE
023459,002255:                                                                                                  #        DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE PRESENT AND DESIRED STATE OF THE ERROR
023460,002256:                                                                                                  #        COUNTERS.  A 20 MILLISECOND WAITLIST CALL IS SET FOR BEGDES
023461,002257:                                                                                                  #        AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM.
