023612,002408:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  BEGDES
023613,002409: 
023614,002410:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023615,002411:                                                                                                  #        BEGDES CHECKS VARIOUS DESIGNATE REQUESTS AND REQUESTS THE
023616,002412:                                                                                                  #        ACTUAL RR DESIGNATION.  INITIALLY A CHECK IS MADE TO SEE IF A
023617,002413:                                                                                                  #        REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) IS REQUESTED OR IN PROGRESS.  IF SO,
023618,002414:                                                                                                  #        CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO STDESIG AFTER ROUTINE REMODE IS
023619,002415:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTED.  IF NO REMODE, STDESIG IS IMMEDIATELY CALLED WHERE
023620,002416:                                                                                                  #        FIRST THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED.  IF
023621,002417:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS REMOVED
023622,002418:                                                                                                  #        AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO RDBADEND.  IF THE REPOSITION
023623,002419:                                                                                                  #        FLAG IS NOT PRESENT, THE CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023624,002420:                                                                                                  #        BIT 15) IS CHECKED.  IF PRESENT, ON EXECUTIVE CALL IS IMMEDIATELY
023625,002421:                                                                                                  #        MADE FOR DODES AFTER WHICH A .5 SECOND WAIT IS INITIATED BEFORE
023626,002422:                                                                                                  #        REPEATING AT STDESIG.  IF THE RR SEARCH ROUTINE (LRS24.1) IS DESIGNATING
023627,002423:                                                                                                  #        TO A NEW POINT (NEWPTFLG SET) THE CURRENT DESIGNATE TASK IS TERMINATED.
023628,002424:                                                                                                  #        IF CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE IS NOT WANTED, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023629,002425:                                                                                                  #        BIT 10) IS CHECKED.  IF NOT PRESENT, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR TO
023630,002426:                                                                                                  #        CHECK RR CDU FAIL BEFORE RETURNING TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.  IF DESIGNATE
023631,002427:                                                                                                  #        IS STILL REQUIRED, DESCOUNT IS CHECKED TO SEE IF THE 30 SECONDS HAS
023632,002428:                                                                                                  #        EXPIRED BEFORE RECEIVING THE RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4)
023633,002429:                                                                                                  #        SIGNAL.  IF OUT OF TIME, PROGRAM ALARM 00503 IS REQUESTED, THE
023634,002430:                                                                                                  #        RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE AND RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE
023635,002431:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 12 BITS 14,2) BITS REMOVED, AND THE DESIGNATE FLAG
023636,002432:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 10) REMOVED BEFORE EXITING TO RDBADEND.  IF
023637,002433:                                                                                                  #        TIME HAS NOT EXPIRED, DESCOUNT IS DECREMENTED, THE
023638,002434:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTIVE CALL MADE FOR DODES, AND A .5 SECOND WAIT INITIATED
023639,002435:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE REPEATING THIS PROCEDURE AT STDESIG.
023640,002436: 
023641,002437:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023642,002438: 
023643,002439:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST CALL FROM STARTDES
023644,002440:                                                                                                  #        TCF BEGDES FROM DORREPOS
023645,002441:                                                                                                  #        TC STDESIG RETURNING, FROM REMODE
023646,002442: 
023647,002443:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023648,002444:                                                                                                  #        DESCOUNT, RADMODES
023649,002445: 
023650,002446:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023651,002447:                                                                                                  #        ENDRADAR, FINDVAC
023652,002448: 
023653,002449:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  DODES
023654,002450: 
023655,002451:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  PROGRAM ALARM 00503 (30 SECONDS HAVE EXPIRED) WITH NO RR DATA
023656,002452:                                                                                                  #  GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) RECEIVED WHEN LOCK-ON (STATE BIT 5) WAS REQUESTED.
023657,002453: 
023658,002454:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_         TASKOVER (SEARCH PATTERN DESIGNATING TO NEW POINT)
023659,002455:                                                                                                  #                ENDRADAR (NO DESIGNATE - RADMODES BIT 10)
023660,002456:                                                                                                  #                RDBADEND (REPOSITION OR 30 SECONDS EXPIRED)
023661,002457: 
023662,002458: 25,2604           40110        BEGDES             CS       RADMODES

023707,002503:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DODES
023708,002504: 
023709,002505:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023710,002506: 
023711,002507:                                                                                                  #        DODES CALCULATES AND REQUESTS ISSUANCE OF RR GYRO TORQUE
023712,002508:                                                                                                  #        COMMANDS.  INITIALLY THE CURRENT RR CDU ANGLES ARE STORED AND
023713,002509:                                                                                                  #        THE LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR TRANSFORMED FROM STABLE MEMBER TO
023714,002510:                                                                                                  #        NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES VIA SMNB IF NECESSARY.  THE
023715,002511:                                                                                                  #        SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS ARE THEN CALCULATED AS FOLLOWS_
023716,002512:                                                                                                  #                + SHAFT = LOS . (COS(S), 0, -SIN(S))  (DOT PRODUCT)
023717,002513:                                                                                                  #                - TRUNNION = LOS . (SIN(T)SIN(S), COS(T), SIN(T)COS(S))
023718,002514:                                                                                                  #        THE SIGN OF THE SHAFT COMMAND IS THEN REVERSED IF IN MODE 2
023719,002515:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) BECAUSE A RELAY IN THE RR REVERSES THE 
023720,002516:                                                                                                  #        POLARITY OF THE COMMAND.  AT RRSCALUP EACH COMMAND IS
023721,002517:                                                                                                  #        SCALED AND IF EITHER, OR BOTH, OF THE COMMANDS IS GREATER THAN
023722,002518:                                                                                                  #        .5 DEGREES, MPAC +1 IS SET POSITIVE.  IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE 
023723,002519:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 15) IS DESIRED AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS NOT OPERATING,
023724,002520:                                                                                                  #        THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT
023725,002521:                                                                                                  #        CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11)
023726,002522:                                                                                                  #        IS IN PROGRESS.  IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS
023727,002523:                                                                                                  #        OPERATING (SRCHOPT FLAG SET) THE TRACK ENABLE IS NOT CLEARED.  IF NO
023728,002524:                                                                                                  #        CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND BOTH COMMANDS ARE NOT LESS THAN .5 DEGREES AS
023729,002525:                                                                                                  #        INDICATED BY MPAC +1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS
023730,002526:                                                                                                  #        CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
023731,002527:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS.  IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5
023732,002528:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES AS INDICATED BY MPAC+1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT
023733,002529:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE
023734,002530:                                                                                                  #        COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN
023735,002531:                                                                                                  #        PROGRESS.  IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5 DEGREES, THE
023736,002532:                                                                                                  #        LOCK-ON FLAG (STATE BIT 5) IS CHECKED.  IF NOT PRESENT, THE
023737,002533:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED, THE RR ERROR
023738,002534:                                                                                                  #        COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED, AND ENDOFJOB
023739,002535:                                                                                                  #        CALLED.  IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED, THE RR AUTO TRACKER (CHAN 12
023740,002536:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14) IS ENABLED FOLLOWED BY A CHECK OF THE RECEIPT OF THE
023741,002537:                                                                                                  #        RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) SIGNAL.  IF RR DATA GOOD
023742,002538:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED,
023743,002539:                                                                                                  #        THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED,
023744,002540:                                                                                                  #        AND ENDOFJOB CALLED.  IF RR DATA GOOD IS NOT PRESENT, RROUT
023745,002541:                                                                                                  #        IS CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
023746,002542:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS AFTER WHICH THE JOB IS TERMINATED
023747,002543:                                                                                                  #        VIA ENDOFJOB.
023748,002544: 
023749,002545:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023750,002546: 
023751,002547:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTIVE CALL EVERY .5 SECONDS FROM BEGDES.
023752,002548: 
023753,002549:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023754,002550: 
023755,002551:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET (HALF-UNIT LOS VECTOR IN EITHER SM OR NB COORDINATES),
023756,002552:                                                                                                  #        LOKONSW (STATE BIT 5), RRNBSW (STATE BIT 6), RADMODES
023757,002553: 
023758,002554:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023759,002555: 
023760,002556:                                                                                                  #        READCDUS, SMNB, CDULOGIC, MAGSUB, RROUT

Page 552 

023762,002558: 
023763,002559:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023764,002560: 
023765,002561:                                                                                                  #        NONE
023766,002562: 
023767,002563:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023768,002564: 
023769,002565:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  ENDOFJOB (ALWAYS)
023770,002566: 
023771,002567: 25,2646           00006        DODES              EXTEND

023826,002622:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDED RATE AND ENABLE THE TRACKER IF WE ARE WITHIN .5 DEGREES OF THE TARGET.

023833,002629: 25,2732           74740                           MASK     BIT12                                 #  THE SHAFT COMMANDS IN MODE 2 SO THAT A

024444,003240:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  LPS20.1 VECTOR EXTRAPOLATION AND LOS COMPUTATION
024445,003241:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO. 2    BY J.D. COYNE   SDC     DATE 12-7-66
024446,003242: 
024447,003243:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024448,003244:                                                                                                  #        1)      EXTRAPOLATE THE LEM AND CSM VECTORS IN ACCORDANCE WITH THE TIME REFERED TO IN CALLER + 1.

024450,003246:                                                                                                  #        3)      COMPUTES THE MAGNITUDE OF THE LOS VECTOR AND STORES IT IN MLOSV

024573,003369:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  LRS22.1 (DATA READ SUBROUTINE 1)
024574,003370:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO.: 1           BY: P. VOLANTE  SDC             DATE:  11-15-66
024575,003371: 
024576,003372:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024577,003373:                                                                                                  #        1)      READS RENDEZVOUS RADAR RANGE AND RANGE-RATE, TRUNION AND SHAFT ANGLES, THREE CDU VALUES AND TIME.  CONVERTS THIS
024578,003374:                                                                                                  #                DATA AND LEAVES IT FOR THE MEASUREMENT INCORPORATION ROUTINE (LSR22.3).  CHECKS FOR THE RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE, FOR
024579,003375:                                                                                                  #                RR REPOSITION AND RR CDU FAIL
024580,003376:                                                                                                  #        2)      COMPARES RADAR LOS WITH LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN THREE DEGREES
024581,003377: 
024582,003378:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BANKCALL FOR LRS22.1
024583,003379: 
024584,003380:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
024585,003381:                                                                                                  #        RRRDOT          LPS20.1
024586,003382:                                                                                                  #        RRRANGE         BANKCALL
024587,003383:                                                                                                  #        RADSTALL        CDULOGIC
024588,003384:                                                                                                  #        RRNB            SMNB
024589,003385: 
024590,003386:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT:  RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH MPAC SET TO +0
024591,003387: 
024592,003388:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS:  RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH ERROR CODE STORED IN MPAC AS FOLLOWS:
024593,003389:                                                                                                  #        00001 - ERROR EXIT 1 - RR DATA NO GOOD (NO RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE OR RR CDU FAIL OR RR REPOSITION)
024594,003390:                                                                                                  #        00002 - ERROR EXIT 2 - RR LOS NOT WITHIN THREE DEGREES OF LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS
024595,003391: 
024596,003392:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  521 - COULD NOT READ RADAR DATA (RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE NOT PRESENT BEFORE AND AFTER READING THE RADAR)
024597,003393:                                                                                                  #        (THIS ALARM IS ISSUED BY THE RADAREAD SUBROUTINE WHICH IS ENTERED FROM A RADARUPT)
024598,003394: 
024599,003395:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:  RRLOSVEC - THE RR LINE-OF-SIGHT VECTOR (USED BY LRS22.2) - A HALF-UNIT VECTOR
024600,003396:                                                                                                  #        RM - THE RR RANGE READING (TO THE CSM) DP, IN METERS SCALED B-29 (USED BY LRS22.2 AND LRS22.3)
024601,003397: 
024602,003398:                                                                                                  #        ALL OF THE FOLLOWING OUTPUTS ARE USED BY LRS22.3:
024603,003399:                                                                                                  #                RDOTM - THE RR RANGE-RATE READING, DP, IN METERS PER CENTISECOND, SCALED B-7
024604,003400:                                                                                                  #                RRTRUN - RR TRUNION ANGLE, DP, IN REVOLUTIONS, SCALED B0
024605,003401:                                                                                                  #                RRSHAFT - RR SHAFT ANGLE, DP, IN REVOLUTIONS, SCALED B0
024606,003402:                                                                                                  #                AIG,AMG,AOG - THE CDU ANGLES, THREE SP WORDS
024607,003403:                                                                                                  #                MKTIME - THE TIME OF THE RR READING, DP, IN CENTISECONDS
024608,003404: 
024609,003405:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024610,003406:                                                                                                  #        RNRAD, THE RADAR READ COUNTER FROM WHICH IS OBTAINED:

Page 575 

024612,003408:                                                                                                  #                1) RR RANGE SCALED 9.38 FT. PER BIT ON THE LOW SCALE AND 75.04 FT. PER BIT ON THE HIGH SCALE
024613,003409:                                                                                                  #                2) RR RANGE RATE, SCALED .6278 FT./SEC. PER BIT
024614,003410:                                                                                                  #        THE CDU ANGLES FROM CDUX, CDUY, CDUZ AND TIME1 AND TIME2
024615,003411: 
024616,003412:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS:  LRS22.1X, A, L, Q, PUSHLIST
024617,003413:

024746,003542:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - LRS22.2 (DATA READ SUBROUTINE 2)

024749,003545:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
024750,003546:                                                                                                  #        2)  CHECKS IF THE RR LOS (I.E. THE RADAR BORESIGHT VECTOR) IS WITHIN 30 DEGREES OF THE LM +Z AXIS

024757,003553:

024764,003560:                                                                                                  #        RM - RR RANGE, METERS B-29, FROM LRS22.1
024765,003561:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14 CHANNEL 31 - INDICATES AUTOPILOT IS IN AUTO MODE
024766,003562: 
024767,003563:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS - A,L,Q MPAC - PUSHLIST AND PUSHLOC ARE NOT CHANGED BY THIS ROUTINE

024797,003593:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - LSR22.3                                DATE - 29 MAY 1967
024798,003594:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO 3                                             LOG SECTION - P20-25
024799,003595:                                                                                                  #  MOD. BY - DANFORTH                                    ASSEMBLY LEMP20S REV 10
024800,003596: 
024801,003597:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024802,003598:                                                                                                  #        THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR EACH OF THE QUANTITIES MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS
024803,003599:                                                                                                  #        RADAR.  (RANGE, RANGE RATE, SHAFT AND TRUNNION ANGLES).  THE ROUTINE CALLS THE INCORP1 AND INCORP2 ROUTINES
024804,003600:                                                                                                  #        WHICH COMPUTE THE DEVIATIONS AND CORRECT THE STATE VECTOR.
024805,003601: 
024806,003602:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
024807,003603:                                                                                                  #        THIS ROUTINE IS PART OF P20 RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION FOR THE LM COMPUTER ONLY.  THE ROUTINE IS ENTERED FROM
024808,003604:                                                                                                  #        R22 LEM ONLY AND RETURNS DIRECTLY TO R22LEM FOLLOWING SUCCESSFUL INCORPORATION OF MEASURED DATA.  IF THE
024809,003605:                                                                                                  #        COMPUTED STATE VECTOR DEVIATIONS EXCEED THE MAXIMUM PERMITTED.  THE ROUTINE RETURNS TO R22LEM TO DISPLAY
024810,003606:                                                                                                  #        THE DEVIATIONS.  IF THE ASTRONAUT ACCEPTS THE DATA R22LEM RETURNS TO LSR22.3 TO INCORPORATE THE
024811,003607:                                                                                                  #        DEVIATIONS INTO THE STATE VECTOR.  IF THE ASTRONAUT REJECTS THE DEVIATIONS, NO MORE MEASUREMENTS ARE
024812,003608:                                                                                                  #        PROCESSED FOR THIS MARK, I.E.,  R22LEM GETS THE NEXT MARK.
024813,003609: 
024814,003610:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
024815,003611:                                                                                                  #        WLINIT          LGCUPDTE        INTEGRV         INCORP1         ARCTAN
024816,003612:                                                                                                  #        GETULC          RARARANG        INCORP2         NBSM            INTSTALL
024817,003613: 
024818,003614:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
024819,003615:                                                                                                  #        CORRECTED LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
024820,003616:                                                                                                  #        NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
024821,003617:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
024822,003618:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
024823,003619:                                                                                                  #        UPDATED W-MATRIX
024824,003620: 
024825,003621:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
024826,003622:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
024827,003623:                                                                                                  #        W-MATRIX
024828,003624:                                                                                                  #        MARK TIME IN MKTIME
024829,003625:                                                                                                  #        RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
024830,003626:                                                                                                  #                RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSES B-7
024831,003627:                                                                                                  #                SHAFT ANGLE IN RRSHAFT REVS. B0
024832,003628:                                                                                                  #                TRUNNION ANGLE IN RRTRUN REVS. B0
024833,003629:                                                                                                  #        GIMBAL ANGLES   INNER IN AIG
024834,003630:                                                                                                  #                        MIDDLE IN AMG
024835,003631:                                                                                                  #                        OUTER IN AOG
024836,003632:                                                                                                  #        REFSMMAT
024837,003633:                                                                                                  #        RENDWFLG
024838,003634:                                                                                                  #        NOANGFLG
024839,003635:                                                                                                  #        VEHUPFLG
024840,003636: 
024841,003637:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
024842,003638:                                                                                                  #        PUSHLIST -- ALL
024843,003639:                                                                                                  #        MX, MY, MZ (VECTORS)

025234,004030: 
025235,004031:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025236,004032:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.4 IS THE ENTRY TO PERFORM LUNAR SURFACE NAVIGATION FOR THE LM
025237,004033:                                                                                                  #        COMPUTER ONLY.  THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR RANGE
025238,004034:                                                                                                  #        AND RANGE RATE MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
025239,004035: 
025240,004036:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
025241,004037:                                                                                                  #        INSTALL         LGCUPDTE        INCORP1         RP-TO-R
025242,004038:                                                                                                  #        INTEGRV         GETULC          INCORP2
025243,004039: 
025244,004040:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025245,004041:                                                                                                  #        CORRECTED CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
025246,004042:                                                                                                  #        NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
025247,004043:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22 DISP METERS B-29
025248,004044:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
025249,004045:                                                                                                  #        UPDATED W-MATRIX

Page 589 

025251,004047: 
025252,004048:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
025253,004049:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
025254,004050:                                                                                                  #        W-MATRIX
025255,004051:                                                                                                  #        MARK TIME IN MKTIME
025256,004052:                                                                                                  #        RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
025257,004053:                                                                                                  #        RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSEC B-7
025258,004054:                                                                                                  #        VEHUPFLG

025396,004192:                                                                                                  #  RADARANG
025397,004193: 
025398,004194:                                                                                                  #  THIS SUBROUTINE COMPUTES SINTHETA = -ULC DOT MY

025459,004255:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME LRS24.1          RR SEARCH ROUTINE
025460,004256:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO  0                     BY P VOLANTE  SDC               DATE 1-15-67
025461,004257: 
025462,004258:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025463,004259: 
025464,004260:                                                                                                  #  DRIVES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR IN A HEXAGONAL SEARCH PATTERN ABOUT THE LOS TO THE CSM (COMPUTED FROM THE CSM AND LM
025465,004261:                                                                                                  #  STATE VECTORS) CHECKING FOR THE DATA GOOD DISCRETE AND MONITORING THE ANGLE BETWEEN THE RADAR BORESIGHT AND THE
025466,004262:                                                                                                  #  LM +Z AXIS.  IF THIS ANGLE EXCEEDS 30 DEGREES THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE IS CALLED TO PERFORM AN
025467,004263:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE MANEUVER.
025468,004264: 
025469,004265:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE - BANKCALL FOR LRS24.1
025470,004266: 
025471,004267:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
025472,004268: 
025473,004269:                                                                                                  #        LEMCONIC        R61LEM
025474,004270:                                                                                                  #        CSMCONIC        RRDESSM
025475,004271:                                                                                                  #        JOBDELAY        FLAGDOWN
025476,004272:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST        FLAGUP
025477,004273:                                                                                                  #        RRNB            BANKCALL
025478,004274: 
025479,004275:                                                                                                  #  EXIT - TO ENDOFJOB WHEN THE SEARCH FLAG (SRCHOPT) IS NOT SET
025480,004276: 
025481,004277:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025482,004278: 
025483,004279:                                                                                                  #        DATAGOOD (SP) - FOR DISPLAY IN R1 -     00000 INDICATES NO LOCKON
025484,004280:                                                                                                  #                                                11111 INDICATES LOCKON ACHIEVED
025485,004281:                                                                                                  #        OMEGAD (SP)   - FOR DISPLAY IN R2 -     ANGLE BETWEEN RR BORESIGHT VECTOR AND THE SPACECRAFT +Z AXIS
025486,004282: 
025487,004283:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
025488,004284: 
025489,004285:                                                                                                  #        SEARCH FLAG MUST BE SET
025490,004286:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS AND REFSMMAT MATRIX
025491,004287: 
025492,004288:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
025493,004289: 
025494,004290:                                                                                                  #        RLMSRCH         UXVECT
025495,004291:                                                                                                  #        VXRLM           UYVECT
025496,004292:                                                                                                  #        LOSDESRD        NSRCHPNT
025497,004293:                                                                                                  #        DATAGOOD        OMEGAD
025498,004294:                                                                                                  #        MPAC            PUSHLIST
025499,004295: 
025500,004296: 26,3442                                           COUNT*   $$/LRS24                              
025501,004297: 26,3442           34755        LRS24.1            CAF      ZERO                                  
025502,004298: 26,3443           55736                           TS       NSRCHPNT                              #  SET SEARCH PATTERN POINT COUNTER TO ZERO
025503,004299: 26,3444           34736        CHKSRCH            CAF      BIT14                                 #  ISSUE AUTO TRACK ENABLE TO RADAR
025504,004300: 26,3445           00006                           EXTEND

025509,004305: 26,3451           00006                           EXTEND

025712,004508:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: R29     (RENDEZVOUS RADAR DESIGNATE DURING POWERED FLIGHT)
025713,004509:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO. 2     BY H. BLAIR-SMITH       JULY 2, 1968.
025714,004510: 
025715,004511:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
025716,004512: 
025717,004513:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR TOWARD THE COMPUTED LOS TO THE CSM, WITH THE CHIEF OBJECTIVE OF OBTAINING RANGE
025718,004514:                                                                                                  #        AND RANGE RATE DATA AT 2-SECOND INTERVALS FOR TRANSMISSION TO THE GROUND.  WHEN THE RR IS WITHIN .5 DEGREE OF
025719,004515:                                                                                                  #        THE COMPUTED LOS, TRACKING IS ENABLED, AND DESIGNATION CONTINUES UNTIL THE DATA-GOOD DISCRETE IS RECEIVED.  AT
025720,004516:                                                                                                  #        THAT POINT, DESIGNATION CEASES AND A RADAR-READING ROUTINE TAKES OVER, PREPARING A CONSISTENT SET OF DATA FOR
025721,004517:                                                                                                  #        DOWN TELEMETRY.  THE SET INCLUDES RANGE, RANGE RATE, MARK TIME, TWO RR CDU ANGLES, THREE IMUCDU ANGLES, AND AN
025722,004518:                                                                                                  #        INDICATOR WHICH IS 1 WHEN THE SET IS CONSISTENT AND 0 OTHERWISE.  THE INDICATOR IS IN TRKMKCNT.
025723,004519: 
025724,004520:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BEGUN EVERY 2 SECONDS AS AN INTEGRAL PART OF SERVICER
025725,004521: 
025726,004522:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
025727,004523: 
025728,004524:                                                                                                  #        REMODE          RRTONLY
025729,004525:                                                                                                  #        UNIT            MPACVBUF
025730,004526:                                                                                                  #        QUICTRIG        AX*SR*T
025731,004527:                                                                                                  #        SPSIN           SPCOS
025732,004528:                                                                                                  #        SETRRECR        RROUT
025733,004529:                                                                                                  #        RRRDOT          RRRANGE
025734,004530: 
025735,004531:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:  TO NOR29NOW, IN SERVICER.
025736,004532: 
025737,004533:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:  (ALL FOR DOWNLINK)
025738,004534: 
025739,004535:                                                                                                  #        RM              RDOTM           (RAW)
025740,004536:                                                                                                  #        AIG             AMG             
025741,004537:                                                                                                  #        AOG             TRKMKCNT        TRKMKCNT = 00001 IF SET IS CONSISTENT,
025742,004538:                                                                                                  #        TANGNB          TANGNB +1       OTHERWISE TRKMKCNT = 00000.
025743,004539:                                                                                                  #        MKTIME

Page 600 

025745,004541: 
025746,004542:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
025747,004543: 
025748,004544:                                                                                                  #        NOR29FLG        READRFLG                (TO 1 AND 0 BY FRESH START) (RESET NOR29FLG TO LET SERVICER RUN R29)
025749,004545:                                                                                                  #        PIPTIME         RADMODES (BIT 10)       (BIT SET TO 0 BY FRESH START)
025750,004546:                                                                                                  #        R(CSM)          V(CSM)
025751,004547:                                                                                                  #        R               V                       (PIPTIME THRU V BY AVE G IN SERVICER)
025752,004548: 
025753,004549:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS:
025754,004550: 
025755,004551:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES (BIT 10)
025756,004552:                                                                                                  #        LOSSM           LOSVDT/4                (= RRTARGET & LOSVEL)
025757,004553:                                                                                                  #        SAVECDUT        OLDESFLG                (SAVECDUT = MLOSV)
025758,004554:                                                                                                  #        LOSCMFLG        READRFLG
025759,004555: 
025760,004556:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  NONE.
025761,004557: 
025762,004558:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT JOBS AND TASKS:
025763,004559: 
025764,004560:                                                                                                  #        INITIALIZING, IF RR IS FOUND TO BE IN MODE 1:  JOB R29REMOJ AND TASK REMODE;  ALWAYS: TASK PREPOS29.
025765,004561:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATING:  TASK BEGDES29 & JOB R29DODES.
025766,004562:                                                                                                  #        RADAR READING:  TASK R29READ AND JOB R29RDJOB.  ALL JOBS ARE NOVAC TYPE.
025767,004563: 
025768,004564: 33,2045                                           BANK     33

025868,004664:                                                                                                  #  LOSCMFLG = 0 MEANS THAT THE DESIGNATION IS READY FOR NEW DATA.  SETTING LOSCMFLG MAKES IT GO AWAY SO SETUP29D CAN

Page 605 

025941,004737:                                                                                                  #  R29DODES:  RR DESIGNATION LOOP FOR R29
025942,004738: 
025943,004739:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE DOES MUCH THE SAME THING AS DODES, BUT A GREAT DEAL FASTER.  IT TAKES THE NON-UNITIZED LOS VECTOR
025944,004740:                                                                                                  #  IN STABLE MEMBER COORDINATES (LOSSM) AND A DELTA-LOS IN SM AXES (LOSVDT/4) WHICH IS 1/2 SEC TIMES LOS VELOCITY,
025945,004741:                                                                                                  #  AND DEVELOPS THE SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS USING SINGLE PRECISION AS MUCH AS POSSIBLE, AND INTERPRETIVE NOT AT
025946,004742:                                                                                                  #  ALL.  THE UNIT(LOSSM + LOSVEL * 1 SEC) IS COMPUTED IN DP AND TRANSFORMED TO NAV BASE COORDINATES IN DOUBLE PRE-
025947,004743:                                                                                                  #  CISION (USING SP SINES AND COSINES OF CDU ANGLES), AND THE REST IS DONE IN SP.
025948,004744: 
025949,004745:                                                                                                  #  THE FUNCTIONAL DIFFERENCE IS THAT R29DODES ALWAYS CLEARS LOSCMFLG WHEN IT ENDS, AND IT STARTS UP THE R29READ
025950,004746:                                                                                                  #  TASK WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED.
025951,004747: 
025952,004748: 32,2550                                           BANK     32                                    
025953,004749: 32,2000                                           SETLOC   F2DPS*32                              
025954,004750: 32,2000                                           BANK                                           
025955,004751: 
025956,004752: 32,2550                                           COUNT*   $$/R29                                
025957,004753: 32,2550  E3,1760                                  EBANK=   LOSVDT/4                              
025958,004754: 
025959,004755: 32,2550           34753        R29DODES           CA       ONE                                   
025960,004756: 32,2551           55106                           TS       TANG                                  #  INDICATE 1ST PASS THRU VECTOR LOOP.
025961,004757: 32,2552           34756                           CA       FIVE                                  
025962,004758: 
025963,004759: 32,2553           10000        R29DVBEG           CCS      A                                     #  COUNT DOWN BY TWOS IN VECTOR LOOP.
025964,004760: 32,2554           54002                           TS       Q                                     
025965,004761: 32,2555           11106                           CCS      TANG
